 In a lengthy letter highlighting India's stand on the border dispute, Nehru wrote that the Government of India is the sole competent authority to take up matters with other governments regarding Bhutan's external relations under the treaty with Bhutan and He has taken up many cases with China on behalf of Bhutan government
 unhone likhaa, 'tibet ke saath bhutan kii seemaa ke sambandh main chini maanchitr main truti main sudhaar kaa maamla aisa he, jis par usee kshetra main china ke tibet kshetra ke saath bharat kii seemaa ke saath charchaa kii jaani he

 The Supreme Court has asked the Muslim board to give an affidavit in a week
 isse purv AIMPLB board kii ore se kapil sibbal ne kaha- teen talaak 1400 saal puraani pratha he or yah sweekaar kii gai he
 This matter is related to faith, which has been going on for 1400 years, so how is it un-islamic
 jaise maan lijie meri aasthaa ram main he or meraa yah maananaa he ki ram ayodhya main paidaa hue
 If faith cannot be questioned about Ram, then why on triple talaq? This whole matter is related to faith
 personal lau quran or haddees se aayaa he
 Will the court interpret the millions of words written in the Quran? Constitutional ethics and the principle of equality cannot apply to triple talaq as it is a matter of faith
 sunwaayee ke dauraan kapil sibbal ne hinduon se tulana kii
 The constitution recognizes the personal law of all religions
 hinduon main dahej ke khilaaf dahej unmoolan act lekar aae, lekin pratha ke taur par dahej liya ja saktaa he
 In this way, this practice has been preserved among Hindus, while in the case of Muslims, it is being declared unconstitutional
 court ko is maamle main dakhal nahin dena chahie nahin to sawaal uthegaa ki is maamle ko kyon suna ja rahaa he? kyon sangyaan liya gaya
 Sharia is personal law, it cannot be compared on the basis of fundamental rights
 hamen har dharm kii samskruti ko sarankshan dena chahie

 mahasoos karaayaa janaa chahie ki ve galat hai or kanoon bananaa chahie

 samvidhan sabhi dharmon ke personal lau ko pahchaan detaa he

 The Supreme Court held an important hearing in the case of advertisements related to gender testing on websites
 supreme court ko tay karnaa tha ki aise vigyapanon par roak lagane se kya soochna praapt karne ke adhikaar kaa hanan hota he? haalanki supreme court ne kaha ki jaankaree praapt karnaa, budhimata or soochna praapt karnaa sabhi kaa adhikaar he lekin ye bhi dhyaan main rakhaa janaa chahie ki isse desh ke kisi kanoon kaa ulanghan naa hota ho
 While the search engine said that withholding such information, it is against the right to receive information
 pichhali sunwaayee main supreme court ne search ingine google, yahuu or microsoft ko ling pareekshan sambandhi jaankariyon ko khatm karne ke liye andruni export cameti niyukt karne ke aadesh die the
 The court told these companies that search engines have to respect and obey the law of the country which prohibits gender testing
 supreme court ne centre sarkaar kii in saamagree par najar rakhane ke liye banaai nodel agency par muhar lagaate hue kaha ki centre ek hafte ke bheetar is nodel agency ke bare main prachaar kar logon ko jaankaree de
 In the first hearing, the Supreme Court had ordered the search engines Google, Yahoo and Microsoft to delete the advertisements on the websites on the gender test in 36 hours
 court ne centre ko aise vigyapanon kii shikaayat darj karne ke liye nodel agency kaa gathan karne kaa aadesh bhi diya
 This agency will forward complaints to the search engines and then the search engines will remove such information and advertisements within 36 hours
 supreme court yah bhi tay karegaa ki kya ye bain 'soochna ke adhikaar' kaa ulanghan he
 The Supreme Court said that such situations have happened that boys are not getting girls for marriage
 ladkaa kaise hoga or ladki kaise hogi? aisi jaankaree kii desh main koi jarurat nahin
 We do not mind whether websites make money or not, but such advertisements cannot be allowed which affect the sex ratio in the country
 ye vigyaapan sidhe-sidhe PNDT act kaa ulanghan hai
 The Supreme Court also expressed displeasure over the Centre's attitude, saying that the law does not allow gender testing advertisements, but it seems that they are allowed in the eyes of the Center
 centre bataae ki internet par maujuud aise vigyapanon par roak kaise lagaayenge?tippaniyan It was said from the Center that the Central Government considers it a violation of law and is making efforts on its own behalf
 vahiin, companiyon kii ore se kaha gaya ki ye vigyaapan hai or act ke tahat nahin hai
 The people of the country have the right to receive information
 bataa den ki supreme court websiton par ling pareekshan sambandhi vigyapanon par roak lagane sambandhi yachika par sunwaayee kar rahaa he
 In the last hearing, the central government had told the court that search engines like Yahoo and Google have prepared a plan to auto block gender-related advertisements and have also removed 22 keywords
